I have had many procedures done with Dr. Omoto.  He is undoubtedly the best oral surgeon in every regard.  With all the surgeries I've had done, I've never had swelling and minimal to no pain.  I know these are normal side effects, however, the better the surgeon, the more likely swelling and bruising occur.  Dr Omoto is extremely talented as a surgeon but he is also extremely kind, calming and explains all procedures completely.  He has patience with questions, concerns and never leaves me feeling uncomfortable about the work being done.
The entire staff is top notch; all are kind, friendly and well trained in their respective jobs.  I've never had to wait long at an appointment and the office is really beautiful and clean as can be.
I should also mention, not that it's necessary, but I've had all procedures done while awake . I know this isn't something most like to do. however, it speaks volumes for the skill of Dr. Omoto,'s skill as a surgeon.

<rate>5</rate>< Review>
Dr Kelly is a wonderful dentist! I have been to many other dentists and he is definitely one of the best!
He explains everything thoroughly and tries to keep as much tooth as possible.
I had gone to another dentist since I was worried about a small crack in one tooth and was told I needed around $4k worth of work done to fix it with a crown.  I decided to get a second opinion as I didn't believe that was needed.
Dr Kelly looked at the same tooth and said it didn't need a crown and could be fixed with a regular filling for a very reasonable rate.
I had a few other issues and got them fixed at the same time. It was quick, easy, and I was very happy with the work that was done.
I had to wait a little while after getting numb as they had a few emergency visits and they very generously gave me a $5 starbucks gift card as an apology for the extra wait.
The prices are extremely reasonable, the staff all very friendly and efficient. The view from the office is also beautiful with the ocean right there.
All in all I highly recommend Dr Kelly!</Review>

Sell some products and supplies too. The only knock I have is how long the waits can be on the weekends. If you'll go at other times it's not so crowded.< /Text>

Deli is dangerously and poorly managed. Meat sliced onto the bare metal of the slicing machine, where other remnant crumbs are there for who knows how long. No deli paper to hold the sliced meat, which is crammed into a plastic ziplock bag and impossible to retrieve without it turning into a disintegrated mess.

Employees seem to be aware of the problems, but say that their complaints go unheeded by management. Store manager tried to blame the employees, but they obviously are not being supported or managed correctly.

Many other visible issues; a call to the local Health Department would likely result in sanctions.

As I have pointed these issues out many times, I will not be patronizing this deli again. Let the manager know if you see the same issues.

The bathroom is positively nasty here, too. Not surprising given it's on Midway, "Home of the Homeless", but at the prices they charge you would think they could afford to take care of the place to at least a minimum standard.

All in all, feh.< /text>
